æ¨æ–‡å†…å®¹:
AMEP provides the first comprehensive framework for analyzing simulation results of both particle-based and continuum simulations (as well as experimental data) of active matter systems.
ç½‘å€:

--------------------------------------------------

æ¨æ–‡å†…å®¹:
The Active Matter Evaluation Package (AMEP) is a Python library for analyzing simulation data of particle-based and continuum simulations. It provides a powerful and simple interface for handling large data sets and for calculating and visualizing a broad variety of observables..

æ¨æ–‡å†…å®¹:
@TheRealFalko A nanomotor of micromotor is a device that converts energy stored in the environment into mechanical motion, typically translational motion. Their linear trajectories are randomized by Brownian motion. The one that rotates is often called a "microrotor".  Hope this helps!
ç½‘å€:
